add_namespace = ireland_events
add_namespace = ireland_flavour_events

 ### CONTENTS ###
 # Intro									(ireland_events.0 -> ireland_events.6)
 # Black Monday / Ulster Comes First		(ireland_events.7 -> ireland_events.12)
 # Pre-Elections							(ireland_events.13 -> ireland_events.20)
 # Elections / Black Monday outcome			(ireland_events.21 -> ireland_events.47)
 # Gateway to the Atlantic / Civil Rights	(ireland_events.1000 -> ireland_events.1499)
 # Focuses									(ireland_events.1500 -> ireland_events.1999)
 # Forpol									(ireland_events.2000 -> ireland_events.2499)
 # Democratic Events						(ireland_events.2500 -> ireland_events.2999)
 # Reactionary Events						(ireland_events.3000 -> ireland_events.3499)
 # Socialist Events							(ireland_events.3500 -> ireland_events.3999)
 # News Events								(ireland_events.4000 -> ireland_events.4499)
 # 1941 Election Tree Events				(ireland_events.4500 -> ireland_events.4999)
 # MIOs										(ireland_events.5000 -> ireland_events.5499)
 # AI Pathing								(ireland_events.5500 -> ireland_events.5999)
 # Hidden Events							(ireland_events.6000 -> ireland_events.6499)
 # Resistance Events						(ireland_events.6500 -> ireland_events.6599)
 # Flavour Events							(ireland_flavour_events)

 # Intro #

country_event = {  # The State of the Republic, 1936
	id = ireland_events.0
	title = ireland_events.0.t
	desc = ireland_events.0.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_great_seal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.0 option ireland_events.0.a"
		name = ireland_events.0.a
	}
}

country_event = {  # Model Republic
	id = ireland_events.1
	title = ireland_events.1.t
	desc = ireland_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_street
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.1 option ireland_events.1.a"
		name = ireland_events.1.a
		add_political_power = 20
	}
}

country_event = {  # George is dead
	id = ireland_events.2
	title = ireland_events.2.t
	desc = ireland_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_death_george
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2 option ireland_events.2.a"
		name = ireland_events.2.a  # Not our concern
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		add_political_power = 10
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2 option ireland_events.2.b"
		name = ireland_events.2.b  # Send a private telegram
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		add_political_power = -5
		CAN = { country_event = { id = ireland_events.3 days = 2 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2 option ireland_events.2.c"
		name = ireland_events.2.c  # Give a speech
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		add_political_power = -20
		country_event = { id = ireland_events.5 days = 2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gave_speech days = 30 value = 1 }
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.3 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Canada gets telegram / hears of speech
	id = ireland_events.3
	title = ireland_events.3.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_gave_speech } }
		text = ireland_events.3.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_gave_speech }
		text = ireland_events.3.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.3 option ireland_events.3.a"
		name = ireland_events.3.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_gave_speech } }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = ireland_events.4 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.3 option ireland_events.3.b"
		name = ireland_events.3.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_gave_speech }
	}
}

 # Black Monday / Ulster Comes First #

country_event = {  # Black Monday (08/02/36, originally triggered by black.1, fires 3 days after BM itself.)
	id = ireland_events.7
	title = ireland_events.7.t
	desc = ireland_events.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_crowd
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {	# Note - please do not remove the immediates / effect tooltips in this event chain, as it can unbalance the minigame if players hold events
		hidden_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_political_power = -30
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_german_eco_dominance_base
				add_idea = IRE_black_monday_1
			}
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.8 days = 5 } #  UDP is pissed
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.9 days = 19 } #  The Empty Factories
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.10 days = 33 } #  The Silent Ports
		#	country_event = { id = ireland_events.13 days = 47 } #  Stitchies & Pinnies - triggered by history
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.11 days = 61 } #  Life Among Ghosts
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.7 option ireland_events.7.a"
		name = ireland_events.7.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_political_power = -30
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_german_eco_dominance_base
				add_idea = IRE_black_monday_1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  #  UDP is pissed. 13/02/36
	id = ireland_events.8
	title = ireland_events.8.t
	desc = ireland_events.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_brooke_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {  # this is to reset pp if the player has held focuses etc
			if = {
				limit = { has_political_power > 43 }
				set_political_power = 43
			}
			activate_mission = IRE_UCF_mission
			add_stability = -0.1
			set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.35 }
			IRE_loyalist_anger_increase = yes
			set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ongoing
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.8 option ireland_events.8.a"
		name = ireland_events.8.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.8.a.tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			unlock_national_focus = IRE_assess_bm
			activate_mission = IRE_UCF_mission
			add_stability = -0.1
			set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.35 }
			IRE_loyalist_anger_increase = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Black Monday 1 - The Empty Factories
	id = ireland_events.9
	title = ireland_events.9.t
	desc = ireland_events.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_alufactory
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -3 }
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -35
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.9 option ireland_events.9.a"
		name = ireland_events.9.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.9.a.tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -35
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # End of UCF. 13/08/36.
	id = ireland_events.12
	title = ireland_events.12.t

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco > 5 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 5 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ww }
		}
		text = ireland_events.12.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco > 5 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 0 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_wl }
		}
		text = ireland_events.12.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 5 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_lw }
		}
		text = ireland_events.12.d3

	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 0 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ll }
		}
		text = ireland_events.12.d4
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 1 }
		}
		text = ireland_events.12.d5
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = IRE_emergency_taxes_idea
			remove_ideas = IRE_austerity_idea
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.12 option ireland_events.12.a"
		name = ireland_events.12.a
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco > 5 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 5 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ww }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = 0.10
		add_political_power = 75
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.35 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_nationalist_discontent_delta = 0.03 }
		IRE_nationalist_discontent_increase = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fullsuccess
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.12 option ireland_events.12.b"
		name = ireland_events.12.b
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco > 5 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 0 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_wl }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 75
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.3 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ecosuccess
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.12 option ireland_events.12.c"
		name = ireland_events.12.c
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 5 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_lw }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 50
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.35 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_nationalist_discontent_delta = 0.03 }
		IRE_nationalist_discontent_increase = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_northsuccess
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.12 option ireland_events.12.e"
		name = ireland_events.12.e
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 0 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ll }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.025
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.3 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fail

		}

		}

	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_obrien
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			if = {	# for some reason the AI doesn't generate the same amount of pp up to that day as a player can
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ww
						has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_lw
					}
					has_political_power < 52
				}
				set_political_power = 52
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.20 option ireland_events.20.a"
		name = ireland_events.20.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			add_popularity = {

		}

		name = ireland_events.23.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_sf_collins } }

			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ecosuccess
					has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_northsuccess
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fail
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_collins_stands_aside_tt
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ireland_events.24 days = 5 } }
	}
	option = {	# Collins stays put
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.23 option ireland_events.23.b"
		name = ireland_events.23.b

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ecosuccess
					has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_northsuccess
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25

			}
		}

country_event = {  # 1937 Election event
	id = ireland_events.31
	title = ireland_events.31.t
	desc = ireland_events.31.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_old_woman_voting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 4

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.31 option ireland_events.31.a"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland elects Sinn Fein with Collins"
		name = ireland_events.31.a	# SF Collins
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = { IRE_sf_influence > IRE_sc_influence }
					check_variable = { IRE_sf_influence > IRE_lab_influence }
					has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_collins
				}
				has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_sf_collins
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fullsuccess }
			add_political_power = 125
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 150 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_remove_elecpath = yes
			IRE_load_sf_govt_advisors = yes
			complete_national_focus = IRE_sinn_fein
			news_event = ireland_events.4000
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.43 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.1003 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.31 option ireland_events.31.b"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland elects Sinn Fein with Mulcahy"
		name = ireland_events.31.b	# SF Mulcahy
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = { IRE_sf_influence > IRE_sc_influence }
					check_variable = { IRE_sf_influence > IRE_lab_influence }
					has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_mulcahy
				}
				has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_sf_mulcahy
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 150
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		add_country_leader_trait = IRE_the_reformer
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_remove_elecpath = yes
			IRE_load_sf_govt_advisors = yes
			complete_national_focus = IRE_sinn_fein
			set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gen_mulcahy days = 20 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.42 days = 5 }
			news_event = ireland_events.4025
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.43 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.1003 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.31 option ireland_events.31.c"
		name = ireland_events.31.c	# SC
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = { IRE_sc_influence > IRE_sf_influence }
					check_variable = { IRE_sc_influence > IRE_lab_influence }
				}
				IRE_sc_election = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		IRE_remove_govt_flag = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_govt_sc_temp
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		country_event = { id = ireland_events.32 days = 5 }
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_remove_elecpath = yes
			IRE_load_temp_advisors = yes
			IRE_dail_eireann_add_sic = yes
			activate_advisor = IRE_dail_eireann_sic
			complete_national_focus = IRE_saorstat_criostuil
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.31 option ireland_events.31.e"
		name = ireland_events.31.e	# Labour
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = { IRE_lab_influence > IRE_sf_influence }
					check_variable = { IRE_lab_influence > IRE_sc_influence }
				}
				IRE_lab_election = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		IRE_remove_govt_flag = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_govt_labour_temp
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		country_event = { id = ireland_events.37 days = 5 }
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_remove_elecpath = yes
			IRE_load_temp_advisors = yes
			IRE_dail_eireann_add_sic = yes
			activate_advisor = IRE_dail_eireann_sic
			complete_national_focus = IRE_labour
		}
	}

		trigger = { tag = GER }
		text = ireland_events.1022.d.GER
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { tag = ENG }
		text = ireland_events.1022.d.ENG
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_riot1
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = { tag = IRE }
			has_democratic_government = yes
		}
		else = {
			IRE = { has_democratic_government = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { tag = IRE }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_mission = IRE_gateway_long_countdown
				remove_ideas = IRE_gateway_long_countdown_idea
				activate_mission = IRE_gateway_short_countdown
				GER = {
					country_event = ireland_events.1022
					remove_mission = IRE_GER_gateway_long_countdown
					activate_mission = IRE_GER_gateway_short_countdown
				}
				ENG = {
					country_event = ireland_events.1022
					remove_mission = IRE_ENG_gateway_long_countdown
					activate_mission = IRE_ENG_gateway_short_countdown
				}
				119 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IRE_gateway_short_countdown_idea
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.1022 option ireland_events.1022.a"
		name = ireland_events.1022.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = IRE }
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = IRE_gateway_short_countdown }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			119 = {
				damage_building = { type = infrastructure damage = 1 }
				damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 1 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = IRE_GER_gateway_short_countdown }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.1022.tt
	}
}

				IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				effect_tooltip = {	# This is done as a tooltip because otherwise the decreased loyalist anger would already be applied, even for non-AN paths, as the government would be PatAut at this point
					set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.1 }
					IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ai = no
							AND = {
								is_ai = yes
								ENG = { is_ai = yes }
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = ireland_events.1150 days = 10 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_engineering_advisors }
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENG decision = IRE_gateway_ENG_construction_113_socialist }
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENG decision = IRE_gateway_ENG_construction_119_socialist }
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENG decision = IRE_gateway_ENG_construction_135_socialist }
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENG decision = IRE_gateway_ENG_construction_134_socialist }
				}
				IRE_remove_early_variables = yes
				remove_ideas = {
					IRE_returning_emigrants_1
					IRE_returning_emigrants_2
				}
				IRE_remove_incompatibles = yes
				IRE_remove_41polpath = yes
				IRE_remove_gatewaypath = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = ENG }
			custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.1050.a.win.tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
					IRE = { is_ai = yes }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = ireland_events.1150 days = 10 }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.1050.a.loss.tt
		}
	}
}

					add_popularity = {
						ideology = syndicalist
						popularity = 0.15
					}
					add_political_power = 50
					add_ideas = IRE_anti_socialist_agitation_0
					add_ideas = IRE_low_legitimacy
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = IRE_disproportionate_loyalist_representation }
						remove_ideas = IRE_disproportionate_loyalist_representation
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.3500 days = 14 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = { custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.1150.b.tt }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_gateway_ENG_totalists
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			IRE_george_gilmore_add_sic_tt = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.20
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_socialist
			effect_tooltip = {
				ENG = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ROOT
						autonomy_state = autonomous_puppet
						end_wars = no
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			add_ideas = IRE_anti_socialist_agitation_0
			add_ideas = IRE_low_legitimacy
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = IRE_disproportionate_loyalist_representation }
				remove_ideas = IRE_disproportionate_loyalist_representation
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.3500 days = 14 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			INT = { add_to_faction = IRE }
			IRE = {
				get_current_government_type = yes
				ENG = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = IRE
						autonomy_state = autonomous_puppet
						end_wars = no
					}
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				complete_national_focus = IRE_scarlet_dawn
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_had_govt_sf_collins }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_had_govt_sf_mulcahy }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_had_govt_blueshirt_coup }
					}
					set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gen_dem_to_syndie days = 20 value = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_had_govt_blueshirt_coup }
					set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gen_EOD_to_syndie days = 20 value = 1 }
				}
				else = { set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gen_SF_to_syndie days = 20 value = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.42 days = 5 }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = totalist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist }
				add_to_coalition = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_had_govt_blueshirt_coup }
					set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_blueshirt_to_totalist days = 5 value = 1 }
				}
				IRE_remove_recorded_govt = yes
				set_country_flag = IRE_govt_se
				IRE_load_socialist_govt_advisors = yes
				activate_advisor = IRE_george_gilmore_sic
				IRE_dail_eireann = { remove_second_in_command_role = yes }
				set_variable = { IRE_legitimacy = 50 }
				set_variable = { IRE_legitimacy_cost = 5 }
				set_variable = { IRE_legitimacy_cost_small = 3 }
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.3525 days = 3 }
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = IRE_labour
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}

		else = {

			IRE_loyalist_anger_increase = yes
		}
	}

		}

				limit = {
					FROM = {

							has_completed_focus = USA_cooperation_treaties

						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.2032 days = 3 }
			}
			IRE_remove_american_guarantee_decisions = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		clr_country_flag = IRE_seeking_guarantee
		clr_country_flag = IRE_joining_faction
	}
}

country_event = {  # Join MA?
	id = ireland_events.2008
	title = ireland_events.2008.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_democratic_government = yes }
		text = ireland_events.2008.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_democratic_government = no }
		text = ireland_events.2008.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes 		### on_action

	trigger = {
		GER = { exists = no }
		has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_IRE_victory
		is_in_faction = no
		NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		OR = {
			has_war = no
			all_enemy_country = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		INT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
		RUS = { has_socialist_government = no }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					RUS = { has_country_leader = { character = RUS_pyotr_wrangel } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_elected_government = yes } }
				has_democratic_government = yes
			}
			else = {
				has_dictatorship_government = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_rejected_guarantee_USA
					has_country_flag = IRE_alliance_refused_USA
					NOT = { country_exists = USA }
					USA = { same_government_type_as_ROOT = no }
					USA = { is_subject = yes }
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_rejected_guarantee_APG
					has_country_flag = IRE_alliance_refused_APG
					NOT = { country_exists = APG }
					APG = { APG_long_in_power = yes }
					has_dictatorship_government = no
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_rejected_guarantee_ACC
					has_country_flag = IRE_alliance_refused_ACC
					NOT = { country_exists = ACC }
					ACC = { same_government_type_as_ROOT = no }
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_rejected_guarantee_NEE
					has_country_flag = IRE_alliance_refused_NEE
					NOT = { country_exists = NEE }
					NEE = { same_government_type_as_ROOT = no }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
				NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
				NOT = { CAN = { has_war_with = WCA } }
				NOT = { country_exists = USA }
				NOT = { country_exists = APG }
				NOT = { country_exists = ACC }
				NOT = { country_exists = NEE }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2008 option ireland_events.2008.a"
		name = ireland_events.2008.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				UKR = { has_country_flag = UKR_small_pact_tree }
			}
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = RUS decision = IRE_join_moscow_accord }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2008 option ireland_events.2008.b"
		name = ireland_events.2008.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				UKR = { has_country_flag = UKR_small_pact_tree }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Volunteer bonuses
	id = ireland_events.2009			### can be triggered by on_actions
	title = ireland_events.2009.t
	desc = ireland_events.2009.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_army_officers

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2009 option ireland_events.2009.a"
		name = ireland_events.2009.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_1
				add_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_upgraded_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_1_monarchist }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_1_monarchist
				add_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_upgraded_1_monarchist
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_2
				add_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_upgraded_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_2_monarchist }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_2_monarchist
				add_idea = IRE_erin_go_bragh_upgraded_2_monarchist
			}
		}
	}
}

						original_tag = SPA

					}

			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_volunteer_bonus_tt_3
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_SCW_volunteers_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = IRE_SCW_volunteers
				if = {
					limit = { is_ai = no }
					if = {
						limit = {
							SPK = { IRE_has_irish_volunteers = yes }
						}
						set_country_flag = IRE_supported_SPK
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							SPR = { IRE_has_irish_volunteers = yes }
						}
						set_country_flag = IRE_supported_SPR
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							SWF = { IRE_has_irish_volunteers = yes }
						}
						set_country_flag = IRE_supported_SWF
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = IMP }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					is_ireland = no
					OR = {
						is_great_britain = yes
						is_claimed_by = IMP
						is_core_of = IMP
					}
				}
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					is_ireland = no
					OR = {
						is_great_britain = yes
						is_claimed_by = IMP
						is_core_of = IMP
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = IMP
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_targeted_decision = { decision = IRE_reclaim_gaelic_lands target = var:133.owner }
				clear_variable = IRE_war_decision_days
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = IRE_monarchist_gael }
					set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_monarchist
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = IRE_regency_gael }
					set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_regency
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
		}

		}

		clr_country_flag = CAN_refused_iedc
	}
	option = {

		name = ireland_events.2018.b	# Stay in ME
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100

				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_sf_collins

					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_sc
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_ndp
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_lab
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_cnat
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_plp
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ENT = {
					tag = IMP
					has_authoritarian_government = no
				}
				GER = { has_authoritarian_government = no }
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_sc
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_ndp
				}
			}
			modifier = {

					NOT = { tag = RAJ }

					}
				}

country_event = {  # 1941+ Elections
	id = ireland_events.2500			### can be triggered by on_actions
	title = ireland_events.2500.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_puppet_govt = no }
		text = ireland_events.2500.d
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_puppet_govt = yes }
		text = ireland_events.2500.d.puppet
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_old_woman_voting
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
		date > 1941.1.1
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_dail_eireann_add_sic = yes
			activate_advisor = IRE_dail_eireann_sic
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = IRE_second_election } }
				unlock_national_focus = IRE_second_election
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2500 option ireland_events.2500.a"
		name = ireland_events.2500.a
		trigger = { IRE_has_autdem_govt = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_elections_autdem
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party < 0.65 } }
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.05 }
			IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_sf_marlib } }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_mulcahy } }
				IRE_richard_mulcahy_add_sic_tt = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_advisor = IRE_richard_mulcahy_sic
					IRE_dail_eireann = { remove_second_in_command_role = yes }
					country_event = { id = ireland_events.2504 days = 5 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				IRE_gearoid_osullivan_add_sic_tt = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_advisor = IRE_gearoid_osullivan_sic
					IRE_dail_eireann = { remove_second_in_command_role = yes }
					country_event = { id = ireland_events.2504 days = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.2503 days = 5 }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ireland_events.2504 days = 15 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_started_41_tree = no }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			unlock_national_focus = IRE_later_sf
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2500 option ireland_events.2500.b"
		name = ireland_events.2500.b
		trigger = { IRE_has_soccon_in_coalition = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_an
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_ndp
					AND = {
						date > 1945.1.1
						NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }
					}
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						has_dictatorship_government = yes
						faction_leader = { tag = JAP }
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = IRE_PATH_SOCCON } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = IRE_PATH_SOCCON } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_elections_soccon_incumbent
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_elections_soccon }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_an_autdem } }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {

				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition }
				if = {
					limit = { has_character = IRE_eoin_oduffy }
					activate_advisor = IRE_eoin_oduffy_cursed_sic ### IRE TEMP - wait for scripted loc fix
					IRE_dail_eireann = { remove_second_in_command_role = yes }
				}
				else = {
					activate_advisor = IRE_john_j_okelly_cursed_sic ### IRE TEMP - wait for scripted loc fix
					IRE_dail_eireann = { remove_second_in_command_role = yes }

			if = {
				limit = { date > 1945.1.1 }
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.2504 days = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = IRE_eoin_oduffy }
				IRE_eoin_oduffy = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = GFX_portrait_IRE_eoin_oduffy_civilian_large_elected }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_IRE_victory }
					IRE_eoin_oduffy = {
						remove_country_leader_role_paternal_autocrat = yes
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								desc = IRE_eoin_oduffy_cursed_coalition_leader_desc
								ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
								traits = { IRE_the_despot_1 }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_an_autdem } }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			activate_advisor = IRE_eamon_de_valera_sic
			IRE_dail_eireann = { remove_second_in_command_role = yes }
		}

	id = ireland_events.2501			### can be triggered by on_actions
	title = ireland_events.2500.t
	desc = ireland_events.2501.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_old_woman_voting
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = yes
		has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep
		NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
		date > 1941.1.1
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_dail_eireann_add_sic = yes
			activate_advisor = IRE_dail_eireann_sic
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = IRE_second_election } }
				unlock_national_focus = IRE_second_election
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2501 option ireland_events.2501.a"

country_event = {  # The Opposition Coalesces
	id = ireland_events.2505
	title = ireland_events.2505.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_autdem_govt = yes }
		text = ireland_events.2505.d.sf
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_soccon_in_coalition = yes }
		text = ireland_events.2505.d.sc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_socdem_in_coalition = yes }
		text = ireland_events.2505.d.labour
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2505 option ireland_events.2505.a"
		name = ireland_events.2505.a
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_socdem_in_coalition = no }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@social_democrat < 0.10 } }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.075
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_soccon_in_coalition = no }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@social_conservative < 0.10 } }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.075
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_autdem_govt = no }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_sf_marlib }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat < 0.10 } }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 0.075
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 0.05
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@market_liberal < 0.10 } }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = market_liberal
						popularity = 0.075
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = market_liberal
						popularity = 0.05
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.025
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.025
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = -0.025
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.025
		}
	}
}

		text = ireland_events.2570.d3
	}
	desc = {	# Steele
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
			NOT = { has_character = NIR_basil_brooke }
			IRE_james_steele = { is_unit_leader = yes }
		}
		text = ireland_events.2570.d4
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_character = NIR_basil_brooke
			IRE_james_steele = { is_unit_leader = yes }
		}
		IMP = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		is_subject = no
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2570 option ireland_events.2570.a"
		name = ireland_events.2570.a
		trigger = {
			IRE_james_steele = { is_unit_leader = yes }
			has_character = NIR_basil_brooke
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
			custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.2550.a.tt
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.2570.a.tt }
		effect_tooltip = { retire_character = IRE_james_steele }
		add_stability = -0.15
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_james_steele = {
				set_nationality = NIR
				set_leader_description = IRE_james_steele_NIR_commander_desc
				set_portraits = {
					army = {
						large = GFX_portrait_NIR_james_steele_army_large
						small = GFX_portrait_NIR_james_steele_army_small
					}
				}
			}
			IRE_remove_basil_brooke_advisor = yes
			clr_country_flag = IRE_brooke_advisor_postwar
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
				IRE_disband_wartime_coalition = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep }
					var:IRE.IRE_former_president = { promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
					IRE_michael_collins = { remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes }
					IRE_michael_collins_add_success_sic = yes
					activate_advisor = IRE_michael_collins_sic
					clear_variable = IRE_former_president
				}
				else = {
					deactivate_advisor = IRE_richard_mulcahy_army_chief
					activate_advisor = IRE_richard_mulcahy_sic
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2570 option ireland_events.2570.b"
		name = ireland_events.2570.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					IRE_james_steele = { is_unit_leader = no }
					has_character = NIR_basil_brooke
				}
				AND = {
					IRE_james_steele = { is_unit_leader = yes }
					NOT = { has_character = NIR_basil_brooke }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_james_steele = { is_unit_leader = yes } }
			effect_tooltip = { retire_character = IRE_james_steele }
			add_stability = -0.05
			hidden_effect = {
				IRE_james_steele = {
					set_nationality = NIR
					set_leader_description = IRE_james_steele_NIR_commander_desc
					set_portraits = {
						army = {
							large = GFX_portrait_NIR_james_steele_army_large
							small = GFX_portrait_NIR_james_steele_army_small
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
				custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.2550.a.tt
			}
			else = { custom_effect_tooltip = ireland_events.2570.a.tt }
			add_stability = -0.1
			hidden_effect = {
				IRE_remove_basil_brooke_advisor = yes
				clr_country_flag = IRE_brooke_advisor_postwar
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
					IRE_disband_wartime_coalition = yes
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep }
						var:IRE.IRE_former_president = { promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
						IRE_michael_collins = { remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes }
						IRE_michael_collins_add_success_sic = yes
						activate_advisor = IRE_michael_collins_sic
						clear_variable = IRE_former_president
					}
					else = {
						deactivate_advisor = IRE_richard_mulcahy_army_chief
						activate_advisor = IRE_richard_mulcahy_sic
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	# IRE becomes independent member of RP
	id = ireland_events.2580
	title = ireland_events.2580.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { tag = IRE }
		text = ireland_events.2580.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		text = ireland_events.2580.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_army_marching_square
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2580 option ireland_events.2580.a"
		name = ireland_events.2580.a
		trigger = { tag = IRE }
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_officialise_cession_of_sovereignty }
			}
			overlord = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = kr_mitteleuropa_integrated_member
					end_wars = no
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			overlord = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_stay_in_faction
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 119 decision = IRE_improve_nationalist_discontent }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 119 decision = IRE_improve_loyalist_anger }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.3450 days = 7 }	# Capstone event
			CAN = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = CAN_within_arms_reach }
						NOT = { has_war_with = IRE }
						NOT = { has_military_access_to = IRE }
					}
					activate_targeted_decision = { decision = CAN_approach_ireland target = IRE }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2580 option ireland_events.2580.b"
		name = ireland_events.2580.b
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_officialise_cession_of_sovereignty }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = IRE
					autonomy_state = kr_mitteleuropa_integrated_member
					end_wars = no
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = IRE
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_stay_in_faction
		}
	}
}

	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.2607 option ireland_events.2607.a"
		name = ireland_events.2607.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_new_constitution_end_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_new_constitution_modifier_tt

		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_new_constitution_temp
				add_idea = IRE_new_constitution
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_will_have_parlrep }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep_postwar } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.2510 days = 5 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_parlrep_postwar_tt
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_federalisation_wip }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = EFFECT_UNLOCK_DECISION_CATEGORY
				NAME = IRE_federalisation
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_federalisation_outcome_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = 113 decision = IRE_federal_assembly }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = 119 decision = IRE_federal_assembly }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = 135 decision = IRE_federal_assembly }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = 134 decision = IRE_federal_assembly }
				set_variable = { IRE_improve_nationalist_discontent_cost = 25 }
				set_variable = { IRE_improve_loyalist_anger_cost = 25 }
				set_variable = { IRE_decision_duration = 15 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			complete_national_focus = IRE_draft_new_constitution
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = IRE_new_constitution_modifier
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_bop_jjok }
				country_event = { id = ireland_events.3100 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = ireland_events.3300.t

		text = ireland_events.3300.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = IRE_aodh_o_neill } }
		text = ireland_events.3300.d2
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = IRE
		has_government = national_populist
		is_in_faction_with = RUS
		RUS = { has_government = national_populist }
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			NFA = {
				has_government = national_populist
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
			}
			PAP = {
				has_government = national_populist
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
			}
			POR = {
				has_government = national_populist
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
			}
			SIC = {
				has_government = national_populist
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
			}
			SPK = {
				has_government = national_populist
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {	# GOC is now da boss
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.3300 option ireland_events.3300.a"
		name = ireland_events.3300.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = IRE_aodh_o_neill } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_goc_kick_out_aodh
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = IRE_monarchist }
				set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_regency
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = IRE_monarchist_gael }
				set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_regency_gael
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			retire_character = IRE_aodh_o_neill
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			IRE_jj_walsh_add_sic_tt = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			complete_national_focus = IRE_the_regency
			hidden_effect = {
				IRE_aodh_o_neill = { remove_country_leader_role_national_populist = yes }
				IRE_jj_walsh_add_sic = yes
				activate_advisor = IRE_jj_walsh_sic
				IRE_gearoid_o_cuinneagain = {
					set_character_as_republican = yes
					remove_second_in_command_role = yes
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = IRE_the_restoration
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = IRE_an_goc_idea_2 }

					}
				}

					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = IRE_an_goc_idea_22
						add_idea = IRE_an_goc_idea_4
					}
				}

					swap_ideas = {

		}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			regional_europe_news = yes
			is_american_tag = yes
			is_ally_with = ENT
			is_ally_with = GER
			is_ally_with = INT
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ireland_events.4000.a

	}

		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }

		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = GER }
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					has_government = national_populist
					OR = {
						tag = BRA
						tag = NFA
						tag = PAP
						tag = POR
						tag = SIC
						tag = SPK
					}
				}
			}
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = { tag = IMP }
			NOT = { tag = POR }
		}
	}
}

	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_socialist_bandwagon } } }
		text = ireland_events.4325.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE = { has_country_flag = IRE_socialist_bandwagon } }
		text = ireland_events.4325.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_news_event_IRE_dail

	major = yes
	fire_for_sender = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { wants_world_news = yes }

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			regional_europe_news = yes
			is_american_tag = yes
			has_socialist_government = yes
			is_ally_with = ENT
			is_ally_with = GER
			is_ally_with = INT
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ireland_events.4325.a
		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
			any_enemy_country = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ireland_events.4325.b
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = ireland_events.4325.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					has_war = yes
					any_enemy_country = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				}
			}
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Country said yes
	id = ireland_events.4550
	title = ireland_events.4550.t
	desc = "[FROM.IRE_investment_response_event_desc]"
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory_construction

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.4550 option ireland_events.4550.a"
		name = ireland_events.4550.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = tooltip_modify_dynmod
			DYNMOD = IRE_dublin_international_hub
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IRE_investment_slots
			value = 0.01
			tooltip = local_building_slots_factor_tooltip
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IRE_investment_industrial
			value = 0.02
			tooltip = local_factories_tooltip
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IRE_investment_milestone
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { IRE_investment_milestone = 4 }
			}
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { IRE_investment_milestone = 9 }
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = ireland_events.4500.t # Name would be weird otherwise
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = electronics
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { IRE_investment_milestone = 14 }
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = ireland_events.4500.t # Name would be weird otherwise
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = industry
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { IRE_investment_milestone = 19 }
			}
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		}
	}
}

 # MIOs #

country_event = { # A check for the H&W MIO to set research speed (donotlog)
	id = ireland_events.5000

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus = 3 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus = 119.building_level@dockyard }

		set_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus = 5 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus = 119.building_level@industrial_complex }
		add_to_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus = 100 }

		set_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus = 9 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus = 119.building_level@arms_factory }
		divide_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus = 2 }
		clamp_temp_variable = { var = IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus min = 0 max = 5 }

		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus = 0.01 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus = 0.01 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus = 0.01 }

		mio:IRE_harland_wolff_organisation = {
			set_mio_research_bonus = var:IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus
			set_mio_funds_gain_factor = var:IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus
			set_mio_design_team_assign_cost = var:IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus
		}

		mio:IRE_harland_wolff_expanded_organisation = {
			set_mio_research_bonus = var:IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus
			set_mio_funds_gain_factor = var:IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus
			set_mio_design_team_assign_cost = var:IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus
		}

		country_event = { id = ireland_events.5000 days = 7 }
	}
}

country_event = {  # Pathing IRE_pick_UCFpath. The flag is cleared after the UCF game.
	id = ireland_events.5500
	title = ireland_events.5500.t
	desc = ireland_events.5500.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1
	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes
	trigger = { is_ai = yes }

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.5500 option ireland_events.5500.a"
		name = ireland_events.5500.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_MULCAHY_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_CURSED_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ww	# Wins the BM game outright
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.5500 option ireland_events.5500.b"
		name = ireland_events.5500.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_COLLINS_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_CURSED_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_wl	# Wins the eco part
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.5500 option ireland_events.5500.c"
		name = ireland_events.5500.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_COLLINS_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_CURSED_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_lw	# Wins the northern part
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.5500 option ireland_events.5500.e"
		name = ireland_events.5500.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_COLLINS_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_MULCAHY_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ll	# Loses both parts
	}
}

			set_country_flag = IRE_elecpath_centrist_couped

		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = IRE_elecpath_radical_couped
			clr_country_flag = IRE_elecpath_radical
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_polpath_abstentionist_an
	}
}

# Resistance Events #

country_event = { # IRA Resistance boot event
	id = ireland_events.6500

	title = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = no }
		text = ireland_events.6500.t1
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		text = ireland_events.6500.t2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = no }
		text = ireland_events.6500.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		text = ireland_events.6500.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_civil_war2

	trigger = {
		is_british_tag = yes
		NOT = { country_exists = IRE }
		NOT = { has_idea = IRE_IRA_UVF_resistance_idea }
		NOT = { has_idea = IRE_IRA_resistance_idea }
		is_subject = no
		IRE = {
			any_core_state = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = annexation_resistance_target scope = ROOT }
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 45
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.6500 option ireland_events.6500.a"
		name = ireland_events.6500.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			add_ideas = IRE_IRA_UVF_resistance_idea
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = IRE_IRA_resistance_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.6501 days = 90 random_days = 30 }
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.6502 days = 180 random_days = 60 }
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.6503 days = 150 random_days = 50 }
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.6504 days = 270 random_days = 90 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Riots in Ireland
	id = ireland_events.6501
	title = ireland_events.6501.t
	desc = ireland_events.6501.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_civil_war2

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = IRE_IRA_resistance_idea
			has_idea = IRE_IRA_UVF_resistance_idea
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.6501 option ireland_events.6501.a"
		name = ireland_events.6501.a
		add_political_power = -10
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = IRE
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = annexation_resistance_target scope = ROOT }
				resistance < 90
			}
			add_resistance = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.6501 days = 90 random_days = 30 }
		}
	}
}

	id = ireland_events.6503
	title = ireland_events.6503.t
	desc = ireland_events.6503.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_bombing

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = IRE_IRA_resistance_idea
			has_idea = IRE_IRA_UVF_resistance_idea
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_events.6503 option ireland_events.6503.a"
		name = ireland_events.6503.a
		add_political_power = -15
		add_manpower = -100
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_great_britain = yes
					is_ireland = yes
				}
				industrial_complex > 0
				non_damaged_building_level = { building = infrastructure level > 0.9 }
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.9
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ireland_events.6503 days = 150 random_days = 50 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # 1916 hidden event (donotlog)
	id = ireland_flavour_events.0
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = ireland_flavour_events.0 days = 365 }
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_spindler_event }
			country_event = ireland_flavour_events.2
			clr_country_flag = IRE_spindler_event
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_1916_entente_event }
			country_event = ireland_flavour_events.3
			clr_country_flag = IRE_1916_entente_event
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes }
			country_event = ireland_flavour_events.4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_natpop_govt = yes }
			country_event = ireland_flavour_events.5
		}
		else = { country_event = ireland_flavour_events.1 }
	}
}

		text = ireland_flavour_events.6.d9
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_GBR_country_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = IRE
		IRE_has_socialist_govt = no
		GBR = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
		}
		OR = {
			119 = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
			119 = { is_owned_by = NIR }
			119 = { is_owned_by = GBR }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_flavour_events.6 option ireland_flavour_events.6.a"
		name = ireland_flavour_events.6.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				ENT = { has_country_flag = ENT_britain_agree_northire }
				is_in_faction_with = ENT
				119 = { is_owned_by = NIR }
				119 = { is_owned_by = GBR }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_war_support = 0.10
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_flavour_events.6 option ireland_flavour_events.6.b"
		name = ireland_flavour_events.6.b
		trigger = {
			ENT = { has_country_flag = ENT_britain_agree_northire }
			NOT = {
				119 = { is_owned_by = NIR }
				119 = { is_owned_by = GBR }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 5
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_flavour_events.6 option ireland_flavour_events.6.c"
		name = ireland_flavour_events.6.c
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = ENT
			NOT = {
				119 = { is_owned_by = NIR }
				119 = { is_owned_by = GBR }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 10
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_flavour_events.6 option ireland_flavour_events.6.e"
		name = ireland_flavour_events.6.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				119 = { is_owned_by = NIR }
				119 = { is_owned_by = GBR }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.10
	}
}

country_event = {  # Canada/GBR has died - triggered by on_actions
	id = ireland_flavour_events.7
	title = ireland_flavour_events.7.t

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_ally_with = ENT
				has_country_flag = IRE_had_war_with_ENT
			}
		}
		text = ireland_flavour_events.7.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_ally_with = ENT }
		text = ireland_flavour_events.7.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_had_war_with_ENT }
		text = ireland_flavour_events.7.d3
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_weeping

	trigger = {
		IRE_has_puppet_govt = no
		controls_state = 119
		GBR = { exists = no }
		CAN = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_flavour_events.7 option ireland_flavour_events.7.a"
		name = ireland_flavour_events.7.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = no
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
			}
			add_political_power = 25
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # WCA wins ACW - triggered by IRE_ACW_end_effect
	id = ireland_flavour_events.8
	title = ireland_flavour_events.8.t

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition }
		}
		text = ireland_flavour_events.8.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				IRE_has_pataut_govt = yes
				has_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition
			}
		}
		text = ireland_flavour_events.8.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_natpop_govt = yes }
		text = ireland_flavour_events.8.d3
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes }
		text = ireland_flavour_events.8.d4
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_WCA_militia
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_subject = no
			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_GER_victory
			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_ENG_victory
		}
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		WCA = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
		}
		INT = { exists = yes }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_flavour_events.8 option ireland_flavour_events.8.a"
		name = ireland_flavour_events.8.a
		trigger = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = no }
		add_political_power = -5
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.025
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland_flavour_events.8 option ireland_flavour_events.8.b"
		name = ireland_flavour_events.8.b
		trigger = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes }
		add_political_power = 25
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.025 }
		IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
	}
}
